SUBJECT: Andrew St. George -- free lance photographer now working
with CBS

8 July 1966
MEMORANDUM
SUBJECT: The Activities of Orlando MASPERRER Rojas
1. Reference is made to a memorandum from this office,
Subject: Plot to Overthrow Haitian Government, dated July
6, 1966, concerning a Livat Farm in the Atlanta, Georgia
ress by an informant who witnessed the "new" of the
the farm for shipment to temporary cache sites in homes
in Miami and Coral Gables, Florida; the pickup of aras
from these homes; their transfer to small boats already
relied to the Miami and Coral Gables. The start of the
docking sites for shipment to Santo Donnaire's ultimate
sites on the Haitian Coast. While the information below may
not be related to the incident reported in reference, the
similarity of the two reports merits attention.
2. A friend of Rolando MASFERRE Rojas told a usually
reliable source of this office that on 27 June 1966
HASFERRE went to a house in Miami where 200 firears were
made to the New accompanied by two American newmen, one of
those vs. the American American press removed from the
pressies by agents of MASFERRE whose faces were covered.
The American photographers took photographs during the
removal of the arms.
3. The same usually reliable source of paragraph two
reported in conjunction with the above that as of early
July 1966, action groups such as the Second Nations! Front
of the Exemplary, ALPHA-66, Comandos-L, and Los Pinos Nuvos,
possessed only small quantities of aras. The only substantial
amount of aras in the area was in the hands of MASFERRE.
4. This information is being disseminated to the Federal
Reseau of Investigation and the Department of State.

HENRI VIXAMAR.)
8. MASFERER SAID THAT HE HAD SENT A LETTER TO THE MAITIAN IN
NASSAU CLARIFYING SOME MATTERS AND REMINDING HIM OF THEIR PREVIOUS
AGREEMENT. IF BY 22 FEBRUARY MASFERER HAD NOT RECEIVED AN
ANSWER TO HIS LETTER HE WOULD SEND LUIS SIERRA LOPEZ TO NASSAU TO MEET
WITH THE HAITIAN AND "LAY THE CARDS ON THE TABLE". MASFERER ADOED THAT
IN THE MEANTIME ATTEMPTS TO RECRUIT 384 TO 449 MEN MUST BE
CONTINUED, AND IN CASE THE HAITIAN EFFORT FAILED THEN THESE MEN
COULD BE USED "IN SOME OTHER WAY". MASFERER SAID THAT HE HOPED TO
HAVE DEFINITE NEWS TO ANNOUNCE AT ANOTHER MEETING TO BE HELD ON THE
EVENING OF 23 FEBRUARY. (FIELD COMMENTS: A CHECK WITH
U.S. GOVERNMENT AUTHORITIES IN MIAMI ON 25 FEBRUARY FAILED TO SHOW
ANY RECORD OF RECENT TRAVEL TO NASSAU BY SIERRA).
9. AT THE MEETING ON 21 FEBRUARY MASFERER ASKED HOMEO LEON
US
FERANDEZ WHETHER THE LATTER WAS READY TO FURNISH 18th MEN FOR THE
INVASION OF HAITI, AS HE HAD PROMISED EARLIER. LEON ANSWERED THAT
HE WAS. (FIELD COMMENT: LEON, A CUBAN EMIGRE, IS A LEADER OF THE
FUERZAS ARMADAS CONSTITUCIONALES DE CUBA EN EL EXILIO (FACCE,
CONSTITUTIONAL ARMED FORCES OF CUBA IN EXILE). FOR EARLIER
INFORMATION ON HIS INVOLVEMENT WITH MASFERER, SEE (C50B-312/82276-65.)
18. FIELD DISSEME: CINCSO, CINCLANT, COMWESTFOR, MIAMI REPS
OF STATE, FBI, CUSTOMS, BORDER PATROL, I&NS, AND USCG (ALSO SENT
PORT-AU-FRINCE, SANTO DOHINGO, MANAGUA, TEGUCIGALPA).
